Soft hyphen is often used in web and in professional print publishing software like Adobe InDesign.

Underline Position and Thickness

Pass

Arabic Typesetting Regular (Arabtype.ttf)

post

underline position and thickness

underlinePosition should be a negative and underlineThickness not 0 or negative.

underlinePosition is '-400'.
underlineThicknes is '20'.

Kerning (kern Table and GPOS Kerning)

GPOS

kern

Simple check if kern feature in GPOS table.

The font has GPOS kerning.

Info

Arabic Typesetting Regular (Arabtype.ttf)

kern

-/-

Check if 'kern' table in font.

Font has no 'kern' table. Please verify if font requires kern table or if only GPOS kerning should be in font.

Info

Arabic Typesetting Regular (Arabtype.ttf)

kern/GPOS

kern

'kern' table and 'GPOS' kerning.

Font has GPOS kerning and no 'kern' table.
Verify with the spec or PM what is required.

Vertical Metrics

Vertical Metrics

Error

Arabic Typesetting Regular (Arabtype.ttf)

OS/2 and head

sTypeAsc/Desc and unitsPerEm

The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender should match or exceed the unitsPerEm value.

The result of sTypoAscender – sTypoDescender (1781) should match or exceed the unitsPerEm value (2048), but it is smaller. Consciously?

Info

Arabic Typesetting Regular (Arabtype.ttf)

hhea

Vertical Metrics

Pull hhea Metrics
